		<div class="title">Batı Trakya Haber</div>
		<div class="titles">
			<div class="scroll">
											<p><a href="https://www.batitrakya.org/bati-trakya-haber/turkiye-cumhurbaskani-erdogan-bati-trakya-turk-heyetini-kabul-etti/" data-wpel-link="internal" target="_self" rel="follow">Türkiye Cumhurbaşkanı Erdoğan Batı Trakya Türk Heyetini kabul etti</a></p>
														<p><a href="https://www.batitrakya.org/yazar/yorgo-kirbaki/yunanistanda-vekillerden-3-ayri-yemin/" data-wpel-link="internal" target="_self" rel="follow">Yunanistan’da vekillerden 3 ayrı yemin</a></p>
														<p><a href="https://www.batitrakya.org/yazar/nikolaos-stelya/yunanistandaki-lavrion-kampi-bosaltildi/" data-wpel-link="internal" target="_self" rel="follow">Yunanistan&#8217;daki Lavrion Kampı boşaltıldı</a></p>
														<p><a href="https://www.batitrakya.org/bati-trakya-haber/yunan-siyasetci-valden-bati-trakyadaki-azinlik-turk-olarak-taninmali/" data-wpel-link="internal" target="_self" rel="follow">Yunan siyasetçi Valden: Batı Trakya&#8217;daki azınlık &#8221;Türk&#8221; olarak tanınmalı</a></p>
														<p><a href="https://www.batitrakya.org/bati-trakya-haber/bati-trakyada-camiye-giren-saldirgan-kuran-i-kerimleri-yirtti/" data-wpel-link="internal" target="_self" rel="follow">Batı Trakya&#8217;da camiye giren saldırgan Kur’an-ı Kerimleri yırttı</a></p>
														<p><a href="https://www.batitrakya.org/bati-trakya-haber/yunanistanda-hakan-fidan-ve-ibrahim-kalin-cekincesi/" data-wpel-link="internal" target="_self" rel="follow">Yunanistan&#8217;da Hakan Fidan ve İbrahim Kalın çekincesi</a></p>
														<p><a href="https://www.batitrakya.org/bati-trakya-haber/avrupa-konseyinden-yunanistana-bati-trakya-uyarisi/" data-wpel-link="internal" target="_self" rel="follow">Avrupa Konseyi&#8217;nden Yunanistan&#8217;a &#8216;Batı Trakya&#8217; uyarısı</a></p>
														<p><a href="https://www.batitrakya.org/yazar/yorgo-kirbaki/egede-sucustu-atinayi-zora-soktu/" data-wpel-link="internal" target="_self" rel="follow">Ege&#8217;de &#8216;suçüstü&#8217; Atina&#8217;yı zora soktu</a></p>
														<p><a href="https://www.batitrakya.org/bati-trakya-haber/bati-trakyada-yunanistana-karsi-turkluk-mucadelesi/" data-wpel-link="internal" target="_self" rel="follow">Batı Trakya&#8217;da Yunanistan&#8217;a karşı &#8216;Türklük&#8217; mücadelesi</a></p>
														<p><a href="https://www.batitrakya.org/bati-trakya-haber/bakan-cavusoglu-bati-trakya-turklerini-hicbir-zaman-yalniz-birakmayacagiz/" data-wpel-link="internal" target="_self" rel="follow">Bakan Çavuşoğlu: Batı Trakya Türklerini hiçbir zaman yalnız bırakmayacağız</a></p>
														<p><a href="https://www.batitrakya.org/yazar/yorgo-kirbaki/abdnin-dedeagac-plani-deniz-ussune-cevirecekler/" data-wpel-link="internal" target="_self" rel="follow">ABD’nin Dedeağaç planı: Deniz üssüne çevirecekler</a></p>
														<p><a href="https://www.batitrakya.org/bati-trakya-haber/bati-trakya-turklerinin-lideri-dr-sadik-ahmet/" data-wpel-link="internal" target="_self" rel="follow">Batı Trakya Türklerinin lideri: Dr. Sadık Ahmet</a></p>
														<p><a href="https://www.batitrakya.org/bati-trakya-haber/iskece-secilmis-muftusu-ahmet-mete-yasamini-yitirdi/" data-wpel-link="internal" target="_self" rel="follow">İskeçe Seçilmiş Müftüsü Ahmet Mete yaşamını yitirdi</a></p>
														<p><a href="https://www.batitrakya.org/yazar/erdem-eren/yunan-milliyetciliginin-tarihsel-arka-plani-ve-politik-yansima-ornegi-olarak-bati-trakya-sorunu/" data-wpel-link="internal" target="_self" rel="follow">Yunan Milliyetçiliğinin Tarihsel Arka Planı ve Politik Yansıma Örneği Olarak Batı Trakya Sorunu</a></p>
														<p><a href="https://www.batitrakya.org/yazar/aydin-bostanci/yunanistanda-12-yil-sonra-ilk-defa-emekli-maaslarina-zam-geliyor/" data-wpel-link="internal" target="_self" rel="follow">Yunanistan&#8217;da 12 yıl sonra ilk defa emekli maaşlarına zam geliyor</a></p>

			<div class="detail">
				<div class="title">
					<a href="https://www.batitrakya.org/bati-trakya-haber/turkiye-cumhurbaskani-erdogan-bati-trakya-turk-heyetini-kabul-etti/" data-wpel-link="internal" target="_self" rel="follow">Türkiye Cumhurbaşkanı Erdoğan Batı Trakya Türk Heyetini kabul etti</a>
				</div>
									<div class="summary">
						Türkiye Cumhurbaşkanı Recep Tayyip Erdoğan Batı Trakya Türk Azınlığı Danışma Kurulu Üyeleri ile Türkiye&#8217;nin Atina Büyükelçiliği&#8217;nde görüştü. Türkiye Cumhurbaşkanı Recep Tayyip Erdoğan, Türkiye-Yunanistan Yüksek Düzeyli...					</div>

						<div class="safirthumb">

<script type="text/javascript">
		/* MonsterInsights Scroll Tracking */
		if ( typeof(jQuery) !== 'undefined' ) {
		jQuery( document ).ready(function(){
		function monsterinsights_scroll_tracking_load() {
		if ( ( typeof(__gaTracker) !== 'undefined' && __gaTracker && __gaTracker.hasOwnProperty( "loaded" ) && __gaTracker.loaded == true ) || ( typeof(__gtagTracker) !== 'undefined' && __gtagTracker ) ) {
		(function(factory) {
		factory(jQuery);
		}(function($) {

		/* Scroll Depth */
		"use strict";
		var defaults = {
		percentage: true
		};

		var $window = $(window),
		cache = [],
		scrollEventBound = false,
		lastPixelDepth = 0;

		/*
		* Plugin
		*/

		$.scrollDepth = function(options) {

		var startTime = +new Date();

		options = $.extend({}, defaults, options);

		/*
		* Functions
		*/

		function sendEvent(action, label, scrollDistance, timing) {
		if ( 'undefined' === typeof MonsterInsightsObject || 'undefined' === typeof MonsterInsightsObject.sendEvent ) {
		return;
		}
			var paramName = action.toLowerCase();
	var fieldsArray = {
	send_to: 'G-JRB0SK7T5R',
	non_interaction: true
	};
	fieldsArray[paramName] = label;

	if (arguments.length > 3) {
	fieldsArray.scroll_timing = timing
	MonsterInsightsObject.sendEvent('event', 'scroll_depth', fieldsArray);
	} else {
	MonsterInsightsObject.sendEvent('event', 'scroll_depth', fieldsArray);
	}
			}

		function calculateMarks(docHeight) {
		return {
		'25%' : parseInt(docHeight * 0.25, 10),
		'50%' : parseInt(docHeight * 0.50, 10),
		'75%' : parseInt(docHeight * 0.75, 10),
		/* Cushion to trigger 100% event in iOS */
		'100%': docHeight - 5
		};
		}

		function checkMarks(marks, scrollDistance, timing) {
		/* Check each active mark */
		$.each(marks, function(key, val) {
		if ( $.inArray(key, cache) === -1 && scrollDistance >= val ) {
		sendEvent('Percentage', key, scrollDistance, timing);
		cache.push(key);
		}
		});
		}

		function rounded(scrollDistance) {
		/* Returns String */
		return (Math.floor(scrollDistance/250) * 250).toString();
		}

		function init() {
		bindScrollDepth();
		}

		/*
		* Public Methods
		*/

		/* Reset Scroll Depth with the originally initialized options */
		$.scrollDepth.reset = function() {
		cache = [];
		lastPixelDepth = 0;
		$window.off('scroll.scrollDepth');
		bindScrollDepth();
		};

		/* Add DOM elements to be tracked */
		$.scrollDepth.addElements = function(elems) {

		if (typeof elems == "undefined" || !$.isArray(elems)) {
		return;
		}

		$.merge(options.elements, elems);

		/* If scroll event has been unbound from window, rebind */
		if (!scrollEventBound) {
		bindScrollDepth();
		}

		};

		/* Remove DOM elements currently tracked */
		$.scrollDepth.removeElements = function(elems) {

		if (typeof elems == "undefined" || !$.isArray(elems)) {
		return;
		}

		$.each(elems, function(index, elem) {

		var inElementsArray = $.inArray(elem, options.elements);
		var inCacheArray = $.inArray(elem, cache);

		if (inElementsArray != -1) {
		options.elements.splice(inElementsArray, 1);
		}

		if (inCacheArray != -1) {
		cache.splice(inCacheArray, 1);
		}

		});

		};

		/*
		* Throttle function borrowed from:
		* Underscore.js 1.5.2
		* http://underscorejs.org
		* (c) 2009-2013 Jeremy Ashkenas, DocumentCloud and Investigative Reporters & Editors
		* Underscore may be freely distributed under the MIT license.
		*/

		function throttle(func, wait) {
		var context, args, result;
		var timeout = null;
		var previous = 0;
		var later = function() {
		previous = new Date;
		timeout = null;
		result = func.apply(context, args);
		};
		return function() {
		var now = new Date;
		if (!previous) previous = now;
		var remaining = wait - (now - previous);
		context = this;
		args = arguments;
		if (remaining <= 0) {
		clearTimeout(timeout);
		timeout = null;
		previous = now;
		result = func.apply(context, args);
		} else if (!timeout) {
		timeout = setTimeout(later, remaining);
		}
		return result;
		};
		}

		/*
		* Scroll Event
		*/

		function bindScrollDepth() {

		scrollEventBound = true;

		$window.on('scroll.scrollDepth', throttle(function() {
		/*
		* We calculate document and window height on each scroll event to
		* account for dynamic DOM changes.
		*/

		var docHeight = $(document).height(),
		winHeight = window.innerHeight ? window.innerHeight : $window.height(),
		scrollDistance = $window.scrollTop() + winHeight,

		/* Recalculate percentage marks */
		marks = calculateMarks(docHeight),

		/* Timing */
		timing = +new Date - startTime;

		checkMarks(marks, scrollDistance, timing);
		}, 500));

		}

		init();
		};

		/* UMD export */
		return $.scrollDepth;

		}));

		jQuery.scrollDepth();
		} else {
		setTimeout(monsterinsights_scroll_tracking_load, 200);
		}
		}
		monsterinsights_scroll_tracking_load();
		});
		}
		/* End MonsterInsights Scroll Tracking */
